glib/gprimes.c glib/gstrfuncs.c glib/gstring.c; do \
          case $f in \
            *.res.lo ) ;; \
            *.c | *.o | *.lo ) \
              sf=`echo "$f" | sed -e 's,\\.[^.]*$,,'`.c; \
              test -f $sf || sf=/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/tmp/t6f4d-0/gettext/libtextstyle/lib/$sf; \
              of=`echo "$f" | sed -e 's,^.*/,,' -e 's,\\.[^.]*$,,'`.o; \
              echo "aarch64-linux-android-gcc -DHAVE_CONFIG_H -I. -I/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/tmp/t6f4d-0/gettext/libtextstyle/lib -I..  -I. -I/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/tmp/t6f4d-0/gettext/libtextstyle/lib -I.. -I/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/tmp/t6f4d-0/gettext/libtextstyle -Iglib -DIN_LIBTEXTSTYLE -DLIBXML_STATIC    -I/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/tmp/t6f4d-0/gettext/libtextstyle/lib/libcroco  -DDEPENDS_ON_LIBICONV=1   -O3 -DANDROID -ffunction-sections -fdata-sections -fPIC -gdwarf-2 -fno-omit-frame-pointer -Wall -Wextra  -c $sf" 1>&6; \
              aarch64-linux-android-gcc -DHAVE_CONFIG_H -I. -I/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/tmp/t6f4d-0/gettext/libtextstyle/lib -I..  -I. -I/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/tmp/t6f4d-0/gettext/libtextstyle/lib -I.. -I/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/tmp/t6f4d-0/gettext/libtextstyle -Iglib -DIN_LIBTEXTSTYLE -DLIBXML_STATIC    -I/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/tmp/t6f4d-0/gettext/libtextstyle/lib/libcroco  -DDEPENDS_ON_LIBICONV=1   -O3 -DANDROID -ffunction-sections -fdata-sections -fPIC -gdwarf-2 -fno-omit-frame-pointer -Wall -Wextra  -c $sf || { rm -f config.h; exit 1; }; \
              sh ./exported.sh $of 1>&5; \
              rm -f $of `echo "$of" | sed -e 's,\\.o$,.lo,'`; \
              ;; \
          esac; \
        done; \
      } 5>&1 1>&2 \
        | sed -e 's,.* ,,' | grep -v '@' | LC_ALL=C sort | LC_ALL=C uniq \
        | LC_ALL=C join -v 1 - libtextstyle.sym \
        | sed -e 's,^\(.*\)$,#define \1 libtextstyle_\1,' > config.h-t; \
    } 6>&1 && \
    if test -f config.h; then \
      cat config.h-t >> config.h; \
      rm -f config.h-t; \
    else \
      rm -f config.h-t; \
      exit 1; \
    fi \
  fi
